<div id="review_1025883972" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1025883972" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1025883972?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/18680917-endless-knight">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Carmel (Rabid Reads) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4295616-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2014">audio-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1025883972" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7160279610587415108"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2014/10/audiobook-review-endless-knight-by-kresley-cole.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>Going into POISON PRINCESS I couldn’t help thinking Young Adult—this is going to suck, but Kresley Cole’s writing quickly won me over to Evie’s side, and then Emma Galvin sealed the deal with her mesmerizing narration. And now, here I am, completely committed to this series, and putting my stamp of approval on book 2. The characters show a level of maturity that I never expected from this genre, and there was even a sex scene in this installment. Yes folks, don’t let the</span>
  <span id="freeText7160279610587415108" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2014/10/audiobook-review-endless-knight-by-kresley-cole.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />Going into POISON PRINCESS I couldn’t help thinking Young Adult—this is going to suck, but Kresley Cole’s writing quickly won me over to Evie’s side, and then Emma Galvin sealed the deal with her mesmerizing narration. And now, here I am, completely committed to this series, and putting my stamp of approval on book 2. The characters show a level of maturity that I never expected from this genre, and there was even a sex scene in this installment. Yes folks, don’t let these teenagers fool you, this is grown up YA at its best. The author does such an amazing job of making readers dislike Death that when the love triangle began to develop I was convinced that nothing could sway me from Team Deveaux. Well, now I’m eating crow because Aric was so skillfully fleshed out that the Cajun is just a distant memory. Jackson who?<br /><br />For a girl that doesn’t want to play the game, Evie sure is racking up Arcana symbols! I love how far she’s come from that scared young woman refusing to accept her new, albeit harsh reality, to the ring leader of an unlikely alliance of Arcana. Greene shows mercy when the situation calls for it, and still believes that more than one power card can survive the coming battle, but when he friends’ lives are on the line, she doesn’t hesitate to do what must be done. I enjoyed witnessing the Empress embrace her powers in ENDLESS KNIGHT; her abilities may be the complete opposite of Death’s, however life can, and does annihilate just as easily. Evie continues to surprise me at every turn from how she deals with the teeth (carnivores), to certain characters’ two-facedness, to Aric’s unexpected past. The Red Queen is no pushover!<br /><br />Coles’ dystopian world-building marched forward in this installment with the Hierophant, Devil, Tower, Strength, Judgment, and World cards. I liked learning more about their tableaux, calls, and powers as well as the characters that they represent. I also developed a soft spot for Scarface, Cyclops, and Maneater—Lark’s wolves. The plot line was uncomplicated: escape Death, and when that fails, survive him. I enjoyed the showdown leading up to Evie’s capture, and her time with Aric was enlightening to say the least. I was happy that Jackson was finally clued in to the game and ecstatic when he and Evie found a brief respite in each other’s arms. But of course, just when Greene decides to trust him his deception comes to light.<br /><br />This novel took so many turns that I did not see coming, and oddly enough, I found myself rooting for the bad guy! Like most other readers, love triangles are the bane of my existence, but the one in ENDLESS KNIGHT is so far removed from what is typical of this trope that I wasn’t the least bit upset by it when it eventually surfaced. I’d mentioned in my review of book 1 that Emma Galvin’s narration carried that installment, so I was relieved to see her flying solo this time around. I’m not knocking Keith Nobbs’ delivery, but I prefer to give credit where it’s due. Galvin excels at bringing THE ARCANA CHRONICLES’ dark tone to life while still doing the youthful characters justice with a YA authenticity that so many performers in this genre lack.<br /><br />ENDLESS KNIGHT concluded with one heck of a cliffhanger, but that’s a recipe for success as far as pre-orders of DEAD OF WINTER go because you can bet I’ll be glued to my earbuds come hell or high water on January 6th, 2015.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7160279610587415108" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17137008082047108452"><b>*1,5 stars*<br/>*Spoiler free review*<br/>* Buddy read with Den & Ella<3*</b><br/><br/>Although, YA and dystopia genres as well as "Hunger Game" kind of plot aren't my cup of tea I really loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13450339.Poison_Princess__The_Arcana_Chronicles___1_' title='Poison Princess (The Arcana Chronicles, #1) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Poison Princess</a>, the first book in this series.<br/><br/>I have mixed feelings about this one.<br/><br/>Even though you can predict from the beginning of the book that there will be a cliffhanger and despite some roll eyes moments, I really liked the first half of the book but not so much the second one.   <i>not</i>
</b> because of the cliffy but becaus</span>
  <span id="freeText17137008082047108452" style="display:none"><b>*1,5 stars*<br />*Spoiler free review*<br />* Buddy read with Den &amp; Ella&lt;3*</b><br /><br />Although, YA and dystopia genres as well as "Hunger Game" kind of plot aren't my cup of tea I really loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13450339.Poison_Princess__The_Arcana_Chronicles___1_" title="Poison Princess (The Arcana Chronicles, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Poison Princess</a>, the first book in this series.<br /><br />I have mixed feelings about this one.<br /><br />Even though you can predict from the beginning of the book that there will be a cliffhanger and despite some roll eyes moments, I really liked the first half of the book but not so much the second one. And <b>
  <i>not</i>
</b> because of the cliffy but because of the "one step forward, two step backward" dance at the end.<br /><br />The book is named after Death —that I really liked— and the story starts right when book 1 ended. The first half was action packed but unfortunately the second part kind of dragged and had some epic WTF moments. <br /><br />A thing I really liked in the first part of the book is that Kresley Cole seems to have decided to avoid the "everybody gotta die but me" kind of plot. Unfortunately, she also decided to go to the typically YA love triangle and OTT crap. <br /><br />The end of the story not only annihilated the interesting parts of the second half of the book, but it also made a total schizo out of Evie. This is worse than any imaginable cliffy.<br /><br />It sadden me to say it but I'm done with this series. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_733862138" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733862138" />
    <a title="Punica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4245526-punica"><img alt="Punica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412096034p2/4245526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/733862138?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Punica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Punica" href="/user/show/4245526-punica">Punica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16175040-endless-knight">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733862138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14400359264007860096"><b><i>DAFUQ JUST HAPPENED?!?</i> What an utter DISAPPOINTMENT!</b> <br/><br/>Especially since I LOVED the first book and was so eagerly anticipating for this one. *le sigh* Everything that I loved from the first book was missing in this one. Instead we get Evie (who I thought was such a badass on the the 1st book) become the ultimate pin-up poster girl for the <b>"YA Female Cliche Foundation- <s>Loving</s> LUSTING Over Two Guys Since Time Immemorial"</b>. Excuse me while I go gag. Yuck. <br/><br/>Seriously!?! This series could have been amazi</span>
  <span id="freeText14400359264007860096" style="display:none"><b><i>DAFUQ JUST HAPPENED?!?</i> What an utter DISAPPOINTMENT!</b> <br /><br />Especially since I LOVED the first book and was so eagerly anticipating for this one. *le sigh* Everything that I loved from the first book was missing in this one. Instead we get Evie (who I thought was such a badass on the the 1st book) become the ultimate pin-up poster girl for the <b>"YA Female Cliche Foundation- <s>Loving</s> LUSTING Over Two Guys Since Time Immemorial"</b>. Excuse me while I go gag. Yuck. <br /><br />Seriously!?! This series could have been amazing but it just had to have a stupid, freaking LOVE TRIANGLE!!! A love triangle ladies &amp; gents. OF ALL THINGS! Good grief. That is the ultimate kiss of death in my book &amp; I can count on one hand the many times I have tolerated this idiotic notion. I, for one, am SO SICK &amp; DISGUSTED with these YA female heroines going stupid over two guys. <i>"I love him but oh, I ALSO love him!"</i> Oh wow, the tragedy. <i>"Whatever should I do?"</i> Hit yourself on the face with a frying pan &amp; wake up, that's what. Ugh. Cannot. Stand. It. And the guys that let themselves get caught up in these kind of situations. *facepalm* Has anyone ever heard of self-respect? How about self worth? No? Huh didn't think so. <br /><br />I could write a "proper" review &amp; explain in further details why I didn't enjoy this book but naaah, It'll just end up making my blood boil. Man, what a disappointment. I am truly saddened I didn't enjoy it because this series could've been my next favorite thing but alas, no. Don't even know if I'll be picking the next one.<br /><br />I honestly couldn't care less now at this point, for what it's worth though, I'm still rooting for Jack. Because Death... no. Just NO. <b>HECK NOOOOO.</b> <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14400359264007860096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2394694080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7954268583308576977"><b>HOT FUCKING DAMN!</b><br/><br/>I'm so confused.. utterly confused. WHO DO I SHIP NOW?<br/><br/><i>Endless Knight</i> just mind fucked me guys. I'm so confused as to who I should believe and I also have no idea who I should be shipping Evie with. Jack was easy to love in the first book but now I have so many questions about him. Then there's Death who I didn't think I was going to fall in love with.. but damn, now I have. I haven't decided if he's my new favorite character because honestly, he's got some tough competition: Lar</span>
  <span id="freeText7954268583308576977" style="display:none"><b>HOT FUCKING DAMN!</b><br /><br />I'm so confused.. utterly confused. WHO DO I SHIP NOW?<br /><br /><i>Endless Knight</i> just mind fucked me guys. I'm so confused as to who I should believe and I also have no idea who I should be shipping Evie with. Jack was easy to love in the first book but now I have so many questions about him. Then there's Death who I didn't think I was going to fall in love with.. but damn, now I have. I haven't decided if he's my new favorite character because honestly, he's got some tough competition: Lark.<br /><br />Evie was awesome and lovable in this book. I had a feeling that when she would "try" and get death to fall for her that she would fall as well. I adored everything about them and laughed so hard when she would try to get his attention. Like washing the wolf. <br /><br />Lark, who was previously mentioned, was hilarious. I loved her snarkyness and sarcasm. I am totally on board with them being an awesome ass duo and kick butt night and day. Besides her, we still get to meet everyone from the first book.. but again, I'm kind of confused on who I should be trusting at this point. Things seemed really off in this book with Matthew and Jack so yeah.. I'm going to keep on thinking and wondering until I dive into the third book.<br /><br />This book added more information about Arcana and I loved every second. Getting to know strengths and weaknesses kept me highly entertained. Getting to learn more about Evie's previous life and how she's connected with Death was eye opening. My mind is currently still trying to make sense of everything.<br /><br />Overall, I really enjoyed this audio and I can't wait to dive into the next one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7954268583308576977" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_482123821" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3MoLnOlvq/ivTyZMGyLnLsZy97GXs76H481MrVxleqZ1N0W8PSqvibhFE2+0n/knZ+uCBsb1/JzsmSRhdbkQqw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YBZJf1ko9tMQtdUfYBTWcLMuAYZYaKZSLw0ScrsHo7nJ6wdfjW3yoge/4DzPqch5Erd0MQku5EkgWXq+ktvJtA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText17912704390587163800" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
